<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Async Await</h3><a id="user-content-async-await" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Async Await" href="#async-await"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">BT: I did not finish the tests, but noticed some troubling things. IE ships AsyncFunction, I believe we should actually not do this</p>
<p dir="auto">SP: im curious why</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: unsure, MM?</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: these is no reason to give it a global name</p>
<p dir="auto">DD: TC39 believes the global isn't a mess already</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: well, because of this, we should take extra care. We should not contribute to the problem</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: we discussed that modules will be a mechanism for us to prevent additional pollution.</p>
<p dir="auto">YK: yes its a risk, modules are a way out of this.</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: GeneratorFunction is not shipped, SES also wants to splice it out. Lets stay with the precedent</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: ES5 added a new global called JSON, this causes grief. Facebook had such a global,</p>
<p dir="auto">DD: Ok</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: does the fact that Edge not ship <code>%AsyncFunction.prototype%</code> at all (that <code>Object.getPrototypeOf(async function () {}) === Function.prototype</code> and should not) mean we need to wait on stage 4?</p>
<p dir="auto">(lots of discussion about whether global topology should block stage 4)</p>
<p dir="auto">...</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: for in order is different we might revert</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: is this demonstrating a problem with that staging process</p>
<p dir="auto">YK: yes</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: im talking on behave a process</p>
<p dir="auto">YK: there is a well known process, feature flags. They have a cost, but the benefit improves the integration process</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: what is it</p>
<p dir="auto">YK: isolate chunks of code (markup) that is isolated, interim work can take advantage of this.</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: the spec is too big</p>
<p dir="auto">YK: what will happen in practice, if AsyncFunction is present. Related work will be able to take into account. There is cost associated for sure.</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: there is an existing cost today, FF has an additional cost.</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: ...</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: I asked the question, because I want to decide how to allocate my time tonight. I didn't want to allocate the time, if the already presented issues blocked anyways.</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: I'll take your word the "cost" is trivial</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: As an implementor, I need to frontload the work that the group feels appropriate</p>
<p dir="auto">DE: it would be optimal to have high quality tests, if there are issues / failing tests we can and judge the risk associated.</p>
<p dir="auto">... deciding core semantics ...</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: 95% confidence interval on "core concepts" or tests related to non-trivial changes. Or issues unrelated to performance/stability.</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: populate visible primordials must be populated</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: this is a hard conversion to have</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: i will report back after tonights</p>
<p dir="auto">DE: various contextual s keywords in edge cases, may have unforeseen complexity. I would like to have this considered a core semantics.</p>
<p dir="auto">SP: risk of shipping, with bugs vs risk of lacking feedback from shipping</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: its a risk forsure</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: That is a good reason why multiple implementations are good, as it they will hope to have overlapping bugs</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conclusion/Resolution</h4><a id="user-content-conclusionresolution-8" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conclusion/Resolution" href="#conclusionresolution-8"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>do not add GeneratorFunction or AsyncFunction constructors to the global object</li>
</ul>
